<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>J.P. MORGAN ACCESS MULTI-STRATEGY FUND II </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>277 Park Avenue </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>New York, New York 10172 </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">August 30, 2021 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Dear
Shareholder: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You are being asked to vote on important matters to be considered at a special meeting of shareholders of each of the J.P.
Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund, L.L.C. and the J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund II (each, a &#147;Fund&#148; and together, the &#147;Funds&#148;) scheduled to be held in a virtual meeting format on September 24, 2021 at 10:00 a.m. Eastern
Time (&#147;Meeting&#148;). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to the public health and safety concerns of the coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic, and to support the health
and well-being of the Funds&#146; shareholders and officers, and other attendees, the Meeting will be held in a virtual meeting format only. Shareholders will not be able to attend the Meeting in person. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The purpose of the Meeting is to obtain shareholder approval for the following two important proposals (&#147;Proposals&#148;): </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(1)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To elect five Nominees to serve as Directors/Trustees for each Fund. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(2)</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To approve a new investment management agreement with J.P. Morgan Private Investments Inc. for each Fund. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You are entitled to vote at the Meeting, including any postponement(s) and adjournment(s), if you owned shares/interests of either Fund at the close of
business on August&nbsp;16, 2021 (the &#147;Record Date&#148;). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Your vote is extremely important, and voting is quick and easy. Everything
you need is enclosed. You can vote in any of four ways: by telephone, via the Internet, by returning the enclosed proxy card by mail, or by participating in the Meeting. We encourage you to vote by telephone or via the Internet, which will reduce
the time and costs associated with this proxy solicitation. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Please vote all proxies you receive at your earliest convenience. </B>Please
review the Proxy Statement and consider the Proposals carefully before voting. Please vote at your earliest convenience even if you plan to participate in the Meeting virtually. This will help control costs associated with conducting the proxy
solicitation and will help ensure quorum is reached, which will allow the Proposals to be acted upon at the Meeting. You may receive more than one set of proxy solicitation materials if you hold shares in multiple Funds or accounts. Please vote them
all. Your vote is extremely important, no matter how many shares you own.<B> </B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Instructions explaining how to vote are provided on the
notice for the Meeting and your proxy card. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you have any questions after reviewing the enclosed materials, please call 1 (800) <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">690-6903.</FONT> We will get you the answers that you need promptly. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>After careful consideration, each Board
unanimously recommends that shareholders vote &#147;FOR ALL&#148; the Nominees in Proposal 1 and &#147;FOR&#148; Proposal 2. </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Thank you
for your attention to these important matters and for your continuing support of the Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Sincerely, </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>J.P. MORGAN ACCESS MULTI-STRATEGY FUND II </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT

<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NOTICE OF SPECIAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>TO BE HELD September 24, 2021 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To the Shareholders: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NOTICE IS HEREBY GIVEN that a special meeting of shareholders of each of the J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund, L.L.C. and the J.P. Morgan Access
Multi-Strategy Fund II (each a &#147;Fund&#148; and together, the &#147;Funds&#148;) is scheduled to be held in a virtual meeting format at 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time on September 24, 2021 (the &#147;Meeting&#148;). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to the public health and safety concerns of the coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic, and to support the health and well-being of the Funds&#146;
shareholders and officers, and other attendees, the Meeting will be held in a virtual meeting format only. Shareholders will not be able to attend the Meeting in person, but will be able to participate remotely as described below. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Meeting is being held to act on the following proposals (&#147;Proposals&#148;), as further described in the enclosed Proxy Statement: </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You are entitled to participate and to vote at the Meeting, including any adjournment(s) or postponement(s), if you owned interests/shares
(&#147;shares&#148;) of either Fund at the close of business on August&nbsp;16, 2021 (the &#147;Record Date&#148;). To participate in the Meeting, shareholders must register in advance by visiting https://viewproxy.com/JPMorgan/broadridgevsm/ and
submitting the requested required information to Broadridge Financial Solutions, Inc. (&#147;Broadridge&#148;), the Funds&#146; proxy tabulator. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Shareholders whose shares are registered directly with a Fund in the shareholder&#146;s name will be asked to submit their name and control number found on their proxy card in order to register to
participate in and vote at the Meeting. Shareholders whose shares are held by a broker, bank or other nominee must first obtain a &#147;legal proxy&#148; from the applicable nominee/record holder, who will then provide the shareholder with a
newly-issued control number. Obtaining a legal proxy may take several days. Once shareholders have obtained a new control number, they must visit https://viewproxy.com/JPMorgan/broadridgevsm/ and submit their name and newly issued control number in
order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. </FONT></P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">After shareholders have submitted their registration information, they will receive an email from Broadridge
that confirms that their registration request has been received and is under review by Broadridge. Once shareholders&#146; registration requests have been accepted, they will receive (i) an email containing an event link and dial-in information to
attend the Meeting, and (ii) an email with a password to enter at the event link in order to access the Meeting. Shareholders may vote before or during the Meeting at www.proxyvote.com. Only shareholders of a Fund present virtually or by proxy will
be able to vote, or otherwise exercise the powers of a shareholder, at the Meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Requests for registration should be received no later
than 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time, on Thursday, September 23, 2021. For requests received after 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time, on Thursday, September 23, 2021, Broadridge will attempt to complete the registration, but may be unable to do so in time for the
Meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Important Notice Regarding the Availability of Proxy Materials for the Special Meeting of Shareholders To Be Held on September
24, 2021.</B> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Proxy Statement is included in this mailing and is also available at <U>www.proxyvote.com</U>. An additional paper copy can
be obtained at no charge by calling (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">480-4111.</FONT> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Your vote is extremely important, and voting is
quick and easy. You can vote in any of four ways: by telephone, via the Internet, by returning the enclosed proxy card by mail, or by participating in the Meeting. We encourage you to vote by telephone or via the Internet, which will reduce the time
and costs associated with this proxy solicitation. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PROXY STATEMENT </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>SPECIAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>TO BE HELD SEPTEMBER 24, 2021 </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_1"></A>INTRODUCTION
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Proxy Statement is being furnished to you in connection with the solicitation of proxies by the Board of Directors/Trustees (each, a
&#147;Board&#148;) of J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund, L.L.C. and J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund II (each, a &#147;Fund&#148; and together, the &#147;Funds&#148;), to be voted at a Special Meeting of Shareholders to be held in a
virtual meeting format at 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time on September 24, 2021, for the purposes described in this Proxy Statement (together with any adjournment(s) or postponement(s), the &#147;Meeting&#148;). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Due to the public health and safety concerns of the coronavirus (COVID-19) pandemic, and to support the health and well-being of the Funds&#146;
shareholders and officers, and other attendees, the Meeting will be held in a virtual meeting format only. Shareholders will not be able to attend the Meeting in person, but will be able to participate remotely as described below. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">This Proxy Statement, along with a Notice of Special Meeting of Shareholders and Proxy Card, is first being mailed to members/shareholders
(&#147;shareholders&#148;) of the Funds on or about August 30, 2021. Any shareholder of a Fund on the Record Date is invited to participate in the Meeting. To participate in the Meeting, shareholders must register in advance by visiting
https://viewproxy.com/JPMorgan/broadridgevsm/ and submitting the requested required information to Broadridge Financial Solutions, Inc. (&#147;Broadridge&#148;), the Funds&#146; proxy tabulator. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Shareholders whose shares are registered directly with a Fund in the shareholder&#146;s name will be asked to submit their name and control number found
on their proxy card in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. Shareholders whose shares are held by a broker, bank or other nominee must first obtain a &#147;legal proxy&#148; from the applicable nominee/record holder, who will
then provide the shareholder with a newly-issued control number. Obtaining a legal proxy may take several days. Once shareholders have obtained a new control number, they must visit https://viewproxy.com/JPMorgan/broadridgevsm/ and submit their name
and newly issued control number in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">After shareholders have submitted their
registration information, they will receive an email from Broadridge that confirms that their registration request has been received and is under review by Broadridge. Once shareholders&#146; registration requests have been accepted, they will
receive (i) an email containing an event link and dial-in information to attend the Meeting, and (ii) an email with a password to enter at the event link in order to access the Meeting. Shareholders may vote before or during the Meeting at
www.proxyvote.com. Only shareholders of a Fund present virtually or by proxy will be able to vote, or otherwise exercise the powers of a shareholder, at the Meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Requests for registration should be received no later than 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time, on Thursday, September 23, 2021. For requests received after 10:00 a.m. Eastern Time, on Thursday, September 23, 2021,
Broadridge will attempt to complete the registration, but may be unable to do so in time for the Meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The most recent annual report of
each Fund, including financial statements, for each Fund&#146;s most recent completed fiscal year have been or will be mailed to shareholders.<B>&nbsp;If you would like to receive an additional copy of the most recent annual report of a Fund free of
charge, or copies of any subsequent shareholder report, please make the request in writing to J.P.&nbsp;Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund, L.L.C., 277 Park Avenue, New York, NY 10172 or J.P.&nbsp;Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund II, 277 Park
Avenue, New York, NY 10172, as applicable, or by calling <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-480-4111.</FONT></FONT></FONT></B>&nbsp;Requested shareholder reports will be sent by
first class mail within three business days of the receipt of the request. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_2"></A>BACKGROUND </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Funds are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> registered management investment companies created exclusively for clients of the J.P.
Morgan Private Bank and J.P Morgan&#146;s wealth management businesses (together, &#147;JPWM&#148;). J.P. Morgan Investment Management Inc. (&#147;JPMIM&#148;) currently serves as investment adviser to the Funds and provides overall administration
services to the Funds. J.P. Morgan Private Investments Inc. (&#147;JPMPI&#148;), a registered investment adviser that primarily services JPWM and its products, currently serves as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to the Funds
and is responsible for providing the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> portfolio management for the Funds. These Funds have historically been housed within the JPMIM funds platform as JPWM
sought to leverage JPMIM&#146;s expertise in managing and administering funds registered under the Investment Company Act of 1940 (&#147;1940 Act&#148;). JPMPI has recently also developed considerable expertise in managing and administering
registered investment companies, most notably in introducing the Six Circles suite of mutual funds (&#147;Six Circles Funds&#148;). JPMIM and JPMPI believe that now that JPMPI is administratively able to manage and administer the Funds, JPMPI should
do so, and that having the Funds managed and serviced through one J.P. Morgan line of business will provide JPWM, through JPMPI, more direct control over the operation of the Funds to best service client needs. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Therefore, in an effort to streamline and enhance the service delivery model for JPWM clients, JPMIM and JPMPI have recommended moving responsibility for
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> operations of the Funds, including portfolio management and overall administration, as well as board oversight, from its current structure to JPWM and the
oversight framework in place for the Six Circles Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">To accomplish this, shareholders of each Fund are being asked: to (1)&nbsp;elect the
individuals (&#147;Nominees&#148;) set forth in Proposal 1, each of whom currently serve as a Trustees on the Six Circles Funds board, to replace the Funds&#146; current board of directors/trustees; and (2)&nbsp;approve a new investment management
agreement between the Fund and JPMPI described in Proposal 2 (&#147;New Investment Management Agreement&#148;), which will result in the appointment of JPMPI as investment manager to replace JPMIM (each, a &#147;Proposal&#148; and collectively, the
&#147;Proposals&#148;). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At a meeting held on July&nbsp;30, 2021, each Fund&#146;s Board, including a majority of the Directors/Trustees who
are not &#147;interested persons&#148; of the Funds (as defined in the 1940 Act) (the &#147;Independent Directors/Trustees&#148;), approved the Nominees and approved each New Investment Management Agreement. At this Board meeting, each Fund&#146;s
Board also directed that a meeting of the shareholders be called to consider approval of the Proposals. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If the Proposals are approved by
shareholders, the following other changes would be made: (1)&nbsp;the newly constituted Board (the &#147;New Board&#148;) would appoint new officers of each Fund, (2)&nbsp;the New Board would appoint JPMPI as each Fund&#146;s administrator (the
&#147;New Administrator&#148;) and (3)&nbsp;corresponding changes would be made to each Fund&#146;s organizational documents. None of these other actions requires shareholder approval. Implementation of the two Proposals, which are subject to
shareholder approval, together with these additional actions, are referred to as the &#147;Internal Reorganization.&#148; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">J.P. Morgan
management believes that implementing the Internal Reorganization and having the Funds be overseen by the Nominees and managed by JPMPI will benefit the Funds and their shareholders in a number of ways, including (1)&nbsp;aligning the management of
the Funds more closely with the Funds&#146; current primary distribution channel, J.P. Morgan Chase Bank, N.A., through the J.P. Morgan Private Bank line of business (the &#147;Private Bank&#148;), and other JPWM platforms, (2)&nbsp;leveraging the
Nominees greater experience and familiarity with the business that serves the Funds&#146; shareholder base, which has been gained through their extensive interaction with JPMPI and experience overseeing JPWM-dedicated mutual funds, (3)&nbsp;ensuring
the continuity of service, and (4)&nbsp;reducing administration fees and producing efficiencies through JPMPI&#146;s assumption of operational and management responsibilities in addition to its current portfolio management responsibilities, which
are expected to result in cost savings for shareholders. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">All actions described above are expected to take place on or by September 30, 2021
(the &#147;Effective Date&#148;). </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>PROPOSAL 1: </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_3"></A>ELECTION OF DIRECTORS/TRUSTEES </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Proposal </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Shareholders are being asked to elect five individuals (&#147;Nominees&#148;) to serve on the Board of Directors/Trustees for each Fund (&#147;New
Board&#148;). In connection with the Internal Reorganization each Fund&#146;s Board has decreased the size of the Board to five directors/trustees and each of the Fund&#146;s current directors/trustees will resign. Each Fund&#146;s Board has
nominated the Nominees to fill the vacancies resulting from such resignations and decrease in the size of the Board. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The resignations of the
current directors/trustees of a Fund and the decrease in the size of the Fund&#146;s board to five directors/trustees are contingent upon the election of three or more Nominees and approval by shareholders of each Fund&#146;s New Investment
Management Agreement as described in Proposal 2. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Funds are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> registered management
investment companies created exclusively for clients of the Private Bank and J.P Morgan&#146;s wealth management businesses (together, &#147;JPWM&#148;). Each of the Nominees currently oversees a suite of mutual funds that are managed by J.P. Morgan
Private Investments Inc. (&#147;JPMPI&#148;) and, similar to the Funds, are offered exclusively to JPWM clients (the &#147;Six Circles Funds&#148;). In light of each Nominee&#146;s knowledge of the business that serves the Funds&#146; shareholder
base and experience overseeing funds managed by JPMPI, it is recommended that the Nominees assume oversight responsibilities for the Funds. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Nomination Process </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Board&#146;s
Governance Committee is responsible for the selection and nomination of individuals for election or appointment as Directors/Trustees, including both those who would not be deemed to be an &#147;interested person,&#148; as that term is defined under
the 1940 Act, of the Funds (&#147;Independent Directors/Trustees&#148;) and those who would be deemed to be an &#147;interested person&#148; of the Funds (&#147;Interested Directors/Trustees&#148;). In evaluating potential Nominees, the Governance
Committee considers such factors as it deems appropriate under the particular facts and circumstances, including, as applicable: (i)&nbsp;the advice of independent legal counsel to the Independent Directors/Trustees as to whether a person being
considered for nomination as an Independent Director/Trustee is &#147;independent&#148; and whether the person is otherwise qualified under applicable laws and regulations to serve as a Director/Trustee; (ii)&nbsp;whether or not the person is
willing and able to serve and commit the time necessary to perform the duties of a Director/Trustee; (iii)&nbsp;the contribution the person can make to the Board and the Funds, considering the person&#146;s business experience, education and such
other factors as the Governance Committee may determine to be relevant; (iv)&nbsp;the person&#146;s character and integrity, and his or her independence, leadership skills and ability to work with the other Board members; and
(v)&nbsp;recommendations from management as the Governance Committee deems appropriate and as consistent with the 1940 Act. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Before
determining that it was appropriate to propose the Nominees for election by shareholders, the Board met with management of the Funds and senior management at JPMPI, reviewed information about the proposed Nominees&#146; qualifications and experience
as trustees of registered investment companies. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At a July&nbsp;30, 2021 meeting, the Governance Committee unanimously nominated each of the
Nominees and recommended Board approval, and, at an August&nbsp;2, 2021 meeting, the Board unanimously approved the nominations and recommended shareholder approval of each Nominee. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Prior to that meeting, the Governance Committee and the Board met to consider this matter. The Governance Committee met separately with its members, in executive session with the Board and independent
legal counsel, and with representatives of Fund management. The Governance Committee plus the Chair of the Money Market and Alternative Products Committee also met with each of the Nominees prior to approving the nominations. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The following is a description of the factors considered by the Governance Committee and the Board in
concluding that each Nominee should stand for election as Director/Trustee of each Fund. The Governance Committee and Board evaluated each Nominee both individually and in the broader context of the Board&#146;s overall effectiveness. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Governance Committee and the Board considered the experience, qualifications, attributes, and skills of each Nominee to determine whether the person
should serve as a Director/Trustee of the Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Governance Committee also considered the overall diversity of the Board&#146;s
composition. The Governance Committee believes the Board generally benefits from diversity of background, experience and views among its members, and considers this a factor in evaluating the composition of the Board. In considering potential
nominees, the Committee values diversity based on gender, race, ethnicity and other attributes. The Governance Committee has adopted a policy on diversity. The Governance Committee expects it will assess the effectiveness of the policy as part of
the annual self-assessment process of the Board. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Governance Committee and the Board considered each Nominee&#146;s commitment to
executing his or her duties as a Director/Trustee. The Governance Committee and the Board considered the contributions that each Nominee would make to the Board in terms of experience, leadership, independence and the ability to work effectively and
collaboratively with other Board members. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Governance Committee and the Board also considered each Nominee&#146;s significant and relevant
experience and knowledge with respect to registered investment companies and asset management. Additionally, the Governance Committee and the Board considered each Nominee&#146;s experience with the Six Circles Funds and business that services the
JPWM shareholder base. The Governance Committee and the Board also considered the experience that each Nominee had with respect to reviewing agreements with the Six Circles Funds&#146; service providers, including JPMPI, the custodian, the fund
accountant and distributors. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Governance Committee and the Board also considered the operational efficiencies achieved by having a single
board for all of the registered investment companies overseen by JPMPI. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Board, based on the recommendation of the Governance Committee,
has nominated for election: Lisa M. Borders, James P. Donovan, Neil Medugno. Lauren K. Stack, and Mary E. Savino, each of whom is a trustee to the Six Circles Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Qualifications of Nominees </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In reaching its conclusion that each Nominee should serve as a
Director/Trustee of the Funds, the Governance Committee and the Board also considered the following additional specific qualifications, contributions and experience of each Nominee: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I><U>Independent Nominees </U></I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Lisa Borders</I>. Ms.&nbsp;Borders has significant
experience in corporate strategy and operations in the public, private and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-profit</FONT> sectors, having served as Chairman of The Coca-Cola Company Foundation, as President of the fundraising arm of a
Level&nbsp;1 Trauma Center and Director of the Health System as well as Vice Mayor in municipal government. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>James P. Donovan</I>.
Mr.&nbsp;Donovan has substantial experience in financial services, financial markets infrastructure and broker-dealer regulation. Prior to his current role as Chairman of a multi-cultural education business, Mr.&nbsp;Donovan held senior executive
positions at FINRA and SWIFT, where he was a member of both the Operating and Management committees. Mr.&nbsp;Donovan also previously served as the Managing Director/Regional Business Executive-EMEA/Japan for Citibank and, earlier, in senior
management roles with other Money Center banks. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Neil Medugno</I>. Mr.&nbsp;Medugno has extensive experience in financial reporting, fund accounting and
fund governance. Mr.&nbsp;Medugno most recently served as Partner of Wellington Management Company, LLP and Chief Financial Officer of Wellington Funds Group, which involved oversight of over 400 funds and over $100&nbsp;billion of assets under
management. In this capacity, Mr.&nbsp;Medugno was also a member of several key firm governance committees. Prior to his roles at Wellington, Mr.&nbsp;Medugno worked in the audit practice of Coopers&nbsp;&amp; Lybrand (now PricewaterhouseCoopers
LLP), with a focus on financial services, including investment management. Mr.&nbsp;Medugno has been determined to qualify as an Audit Committee Financial Expert for each of the Funds. The Board believes Mr.&nbsp;Medugno&#146;s experience,
qualifications, attributes or skills, on an individual basis and in combination with those of the other Trustees, lead to the conclusion that he possesses the requisite skills and attributes to carry out oversight responsibilities as Audit Committee
Financial Expert for each of the Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Lauren Stack</I>. Ms.&nbsp;Stack has significant corporate and executive leadership experience,
most recently joining HyperSpectral APD (a physics/machine learning company focused on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> testing) as Head of Operations. She also serves as a principal at a private consulting services firm and as
trustee of a college savings plan. Prior to these roles, Ms.&nbsp;Stack served as Chief Operating Officer of a professional services firm and a privately funded museum/college with responsibility for a range of operations, including finance, audit,
legal and business development activities. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I><U>Interested Nominee </U></I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>Mary Savino</I>. Ms.&nbsp;Savino has over 25 years of experience in financial services and extensive experience with registered investment companies. She began her career in mutual funds at Morgan
Stanley, where she held several positions in the mutual fund group formerly known as The Pierpont Funds until the team was acquired by Morgan Guaranty Trust Company in 1988. After joining J.P. Morgan, Ms.&nbsp;Savino held various roles of increasing
responsibility within the Asset&nbsp;&amp; Wealth Management business, including Head of US Mutual Funds. Since 2016, Ms.&nbsp;Savino serves as the Head of Investment Advisory for JPMPI, where she provides strategic guidance on investment adviser
activities. Between 2009 and 2016, she served as Global Head of the Portfolio Management Group and Global Head of Client Portfolio Management for the Global Access Funds. Ms.&nbsp;Savino has extensive experience in the management and operations of
funds, product development, marketing, sales and regulatory matters. Ms.&nbsp;Savino would be an &#147;interested&#148; Director/Trustee based on current employment by JPMPI. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The current directors/trustees of the Funds are John F. Finn, Stephen P. Fisher, Kathleen M. Gallagher, Frankie D. Hughes, Raymond Kanner, Mary E. Martinez, Marilyn McCoy, Dr. Robert A. Oden, Jr. and
Marian U. Pardo (collectively, the &#147;Current Directors/Trustees&#148;). No information regarding the experience, qualifications, attributes, or skills of the directors/trustees is provided for the Current Directors/Trustees because their term of
office will not continue if the shareholders approve the Nominees for election as Directors/Trustees. </FONT></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Each Nominee, if elected, would serve for an indefinite term, subject to the Funds&#146; retirement policy, which is
expected to be set at age 75 for all Directors/Trustees. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">It is the intention of the persons named in the enclosed Proxy, unless instructed by
Proxy to withhold authority to vote for the Nominees, to vote all validly executed Proxies for the election of the Nominees. Should any of the Nominees become unable or unwilling to accept nomination or election, the persons named in the Proxy will
exercise their voting power in favor of such person or persons as the Board may recommend or, in the case of the Independent Director/Trustee Nominee, as Independent Director/Trustee of the Funds may recommend. All of the Nominees have consented to
being named in this Proxy Statement and to serve if elected. The Funds know of no reason why any of the Nominees would be unable or unwilling to accept nomination or election. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Board Leadership Structure and Oversight </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If the Proposals are approved, the Funds expect
the New Board to adopt the same Board leadership structure and oversight roles as are in place for the Six Circles Funds Board, which are described below. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">8 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Specifically, it is the expectation that the New Board will structure itself in a manner it believes allows
it to effectively perform its oversight function. The New Board has indicated the following: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At least a majority of the New Board will be
comprised of Directors/Trustees who are Independent Directors/Trustees, which generally are Trustees who are not affiliated with JPMPI, the principal underwriter, or their affiliates. The Chairman of the New Board will be an Interested Trustee. The
New Board will designate a Lead Independent Director/Trustee to provide an effective independent voice in the leadership structure. The Lead Independent Director/Trustee will: (i)&nbsp;preside over board meetings in the absence of the Chairman of
the New Board; (ii)&nbsp;preside over executive sessions of the Independent Directors/Trustees; (iii)&nbsp;along with the Chairman of the New Board, oversee the development of agendas for Board meetings; (iv)&nbsp;facilitate dealings and
communications between the Independent Directors/Trustees and management, and among the Independent Directors/Trustees; and (v)&nbsp;have such other responsibilities as the New Board or the Independent Directors/Trustees determine from time to time.
The New Board will adopt a committee structure that it believes will allow it to effectively perform its oversight function for all of the funds in the complex. The New Board will have two standing committees: the Audit Committee and the Governance
and Nominating Committee (each, a &#147;Committee&#148; and collectively, the &#147;Committees&#148;). See &#147;Board Leadership Structure and Oversight&#148; and &#147;Appendix A&#151;Descriptions of Committees of the New Board.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The New Board and its Committees will take an active role in risk oversight, including the risks associated with registered investment companies, such as
investment risk, compliance and valuation. In addition, in connection with its oversight function, the New Board will receive regular reports from the funds&#146; Chief Compliance Officer, Principal Financial Officer and Treasurer, the adviser, the
administrator, and the internal audit department of JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp; Co. The New Board will also receive periodic reports from a risk officer at JPMPI, including reports concerning operational controls that the New Board believes are
designed to address market risk, credit risk, and liquidity risk, among others. The New Board will also receive regular reports from personnel responsible for JPMPI&#146;s business resiliency and disaster recovery. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In addition, the New Board and its Committees will work on an ongoing basis to fulfill the oversight function. The Audit Committee is responsible for
oversight of the performance of the funds&#146; audit, accounting and financial reporting policies, practices and internal controls, overseeing the quality and objectivity of the funds&#146; independent audit and the financial statements of the
funds, and acting as a liaison between the funds&#146; independent registered public accounting firm and the full New Board. The Governance and Nominating Committee will be responsible for, among other things, oversight of matters relating to the
funds&#146; corporate governance obligations, fund service providers and litigation. At each periodic meeting, each of the Governance and Nominating Committee and the Audit Committee will report their committee proceedings to the full New Board. It
is expected that this Committee structure will allow the New Board to efficiently evaluate a large amount of material and effectively fulfill its oversight function. Annually, the New Board will consider the efficiency of this committee structure.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Equity Securities Owned by Directors/Trustees/Nominees </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As of June&nbsp;30, 2021. the Nominees did not beneficially own any equity securities of the Funds. The Nominees do not beneficially own any equity securities in any of the funds they currently oversee,
as the Nominees are not technically eligible investors of the funds they currently oversee. No information regarding ownership of equity securities owned by the current Directors/Trustees is provided for the current Directors/Trustees, whose term of
office will not continue if the shareholders approve the Nominees for election as Directors/Trustees. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As to each Nominee and his or her
immediate family members, no person owned beneficially or of record securities in JPMIM or any principal underwriter of the Funds, or a person (other than a registered investment company) directly or indirectly controlling, controlled by or under
common control with JPMIM or any principal underwriter of the Funds as of December&nbsp;31, 2020. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">9 </FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">As of June&nbsp;30, 2021, the aggregate number of interests/shares (&#147;shares&#148;) of the Funds owned
by the Fund&#146;s current officers, current Directors/Trustees, Nominees and MSFMM, Inc., the current Managing Member (the &#147;Managing Member&#148;) of J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund, L.L.C. as a group was less than 1% of each
Fund&#146;s outstanding shares. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Proposed Officers of the Funds </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Below is information on the proposed officers of the Funds who will take office as of the Effective Date with respect to the Funds in the event that Fund shareholders approve the Proposals. Shareholders
are not being asked to vote on the proposed officers of the Funds. If elected, the New Board will appoint the officers of the Funds. The contact address for each of the officers, unless otherwise noted, is 383 Madison Avenue, New York, NY 10179.
