 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">C-9
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_11"></A>APPENDIX D </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>FORM OF </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>INVESTMENT MANAGEMENT AGREEMENT </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>J.P. MORGAN ACCESS
MULTI-STRATEGY FUND II </U></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>INVESTMENT MANAGEMENT AGREEMENT </U></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">INVESTMENT MANAGEMENT AGREEMENT to be effective as of the [&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]day of
[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;], 20[&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;]between J.P. MORGAN ACCESS MULTI-STRATEGY FUND, II, a Delaware statutory trust (the &#147;Fund&#148;), and J.P. MORGAN PRIVATE INVESTMENTS
MANAGEMENT INC., a Delaware corporation (the &#147;Investment Manager&#148;). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">WHEREAS, the Fund has been organized for the
purpose of allocating discrete pools of its capital among portfolio managers (the &#147;Portfolio Managers&#148;) that invest through investment pools or managed accounts in a variety of markets and that employ, as a group, a range of investment
techniques and strategies, as described in the Confidential Private Placement Memorandum of the Fund, as it may be amended and supplemented from time to time (the &#147;Private Placement Memorandum&#148;), and the Fund desires to avail itself of the
experience, sources of information, advice, assistance and facilities of the Investment Manager, and desires to have the Investment Manager perform for it various investment management services; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">WHEREAS, the Investment Manager is willing to perform such services under the terms and conditions hereinafter set forth; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">WHEREAS, the Investment Manager has received a copy of the Agreement and Declaration of Trust (&#147;Declaration of Trust&#148;) of the
Fund, in effect as of the date of this Agreement, and the Private Placement Memorandum; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of
the mutual covenants herein contained and for other good and valuable consideration the receipt whereof is hereby acknowledged, the parties hereto agree as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.&nbsp;<U>Appointment of the Investment Manager</U>. The Investment Manager will act as investment manager to the Fund and will be responsible for all investment decisions, either directly or indirectly
through the selection and monitoring of the Portfolio Managers through which the assets of the Fund will be invested. The Investment Manager undertakes to give the Fund the benefit of its best judgment, efforts and facilities in rendering its
services. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.&nbsp;<U>Authority of the Investment Manager</U>. Subject to Section&nbsp;5, and in connection with its
obligations under this Agreement, the Investment Manager will have the authority for and in the name of the Fund (including, to the extent applicable, any subsidiary of the Fund) to manage the investment and reinvestment of the assets of the Fund
and to continuously review, supervise and administer the investment program of the Fund subject to oversight by the Fund&#146;s Board of Trustees (the &#147;Board of Trustees&#148;) and in accordance with the investment objective and policies
described in the Private Placement Memorandum. Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, the Investment Manager is specifically authorized to: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) invest discrete portions of the Fund&#146;s assets (which may constitute, in the aggregate, all of the Fund&#146;s assets) in unregistered investment funds or other investment vehicles and registered
investment companies (&#147;Investment Funds&#148;) that are managed by Portfolio Managers, which investments shall be subject in each case to the terms and conditions of the respective governing documents utilized by each Portfolio Manager;
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) invest the Fund&#146;s assets in any type of instrument it deems appropriate for the purpose of fulfilling
the investment objective of the Fund as described in the Private Placement Memorandum; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-1
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c) invest the cash balances of the Fund in any instruments it deems
appropriate and to reinvest any income earned thereon in accordance with the investment program of the Fund; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d) borrow or raise monies, on behalf of the Fund, and, from time to time issue, accept, endorse and execute promissory
notes, drafts, bills of exchange, warrants, bonds, debentures and other negotiable or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-negotiable</FONT> instruments and evidences of indebtedness, and secure the payment of such or other obligations by mortgage
upon, or hypothecation or pledge of, all or part of the property of the Fund, whether at the time owned or thereafter acquired, when deemed appropriate by the Investment Manager, including, without limitation, to meet repurchases that would
otherwise result in the premature liquidation of investments; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(e) open, maintain and close bank accounts and
brokerage accounts in the name of the Fund and draw checks or other orders for the payment of monies in respect of those accounts, and issue instructions and authorizations to brokers regarding securities and/or money therein, subject to the
oversight of the Board of Trustees; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(f) maintain books and records with respect to the Fund&#146;s
transactions and shall render to the Fund&#146;s Board of Directors such periodic and special reports as the Directors may reasonably request; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(g) do any and all acts on behalf of the Fund, and exercise all rights of the Fund, with respect to its interest in any person, firm, corporation or other entity, including, without limitation, the voting
or abstention from voting of limited liability company interests, limited partnership interests, shares or other interests of the Investment Funds, participation in arrangements with creditors, the institution and settlement or compromise of suits
and administrative proceedings and other like or similar matters; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(h) advise the Board of Trustees in
connection with any proposed changes to the Fund&#146;s investment guidelines, policies or strategies from time to time in order to meet the Fund&#146;s investment objective; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(i) supply the Fund&#146;s administrator, custodian, escrow agent, or other service providers to the Fund, with such
information and instructions as may be necessary to enable such person or persons to perform their duties in accordance with the applicable agreements; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(j) authorize any employee or other agent of the Investment Manager or agent or employee of the Fund to act for and on behalf of the Fund in all matters incidental to the foregoing; and </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(k) engage personnel, whether part-time or full-time, attorneys and independent accountants or such other persons as the
Investment Manager may deem necessary or advisable. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(l) engage assistance in performing its services hereunder
by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-managers,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisors</FONT> or consultants that it selects. As such, it is understood and agreed that the Investment Manager may from time to time employ or associate
with such other entities or persons as the Investment Manager believes appropriate to assist in the performance of this Agreement with respect to the Fund (each a &#147;Subadviser&#148;), and that any such Subadviser shall have all of the rights and
powers of the Investment Manager set forth in this Agreement as with respect to the Fund; <I>provided,</I> that a Fund shall not pay any compensation beyond the compensation payable to the Investment Manager under this Agreement for the services
provided by any Subadviser, and the Investment Manager shall be as fully responsible to the Fund for the acts and omissions of the Subadviser as it is for its own acts and omissions, unless otherwise agreed by the parties; and <I>provided
further,</I> that unless the Fund acts in reliance on exemptive, interpretive or other relief granted by the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) from the provisions of the Investment Company Act of 1940 (the &#147;1940
Act&#148;) requiring such approval by security holders, the retention of any Subadviser, shall be approved in advance by (i)&nbsp;the Board of Directors and (ii)&nbsp;vote of a majority of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund pursuant to
provisions of the 1940 Act requiring such approval unless the Fund acts in reliance on exemptive, interpretive or other relief granted by the SEC. The Investment Manager will review, monitor and report to the Board of Directors regarding the
performance and investment procedures of any Subadviser. In the event that the services of any Subadviser are terminated, the Investment Manager may provide investment advisory services pursuant to this Agreement to the Fund without a Subadviser and
</FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-2
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
without further shareholder approval to the extent consistent with the 1940 Act. A Subadviser may be an affiliate of the Investment Manager. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3.&nbsp;<U>Policies of the Fund</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The activities engaged in by the Investment Manager on behalf of the Fund shall be subject to the policies and control of the Board of Trustees. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) The Fund and the Investment Manager agree to furnish to each other current prospectuses, proxy statements, reports to
members or shareholders, true and complete copies of their financial statements, and such other information with regard to their affairs as each may reasonably request. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4.&nbsp;<U>Status of the Investment Manager</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The
Investment Manager will for all purposes be an independent contractor and not an employee of the Fund, nor will anything in this Agreement be construed as making the Fund a partner or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-venturer</FONT> with the
Investment Manager or any of its affiliates or clients. The Investment Manager shall have no authority to act for, represent, bind or obligate the Fund except as specifically provided in this Agreement or as specifically approved by the Board of
Trustees. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) The Fund authorizes affiliates of the Investment Manager to provide services relating to the
investment or trading of securities for the Fund and to retain compensation in connection with the transactions, provided that any such affiliate discloses, at least annually, and as may be required under the Fund&#146;s Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17e-1</FONT> Procedures, as amended from time to time with notice to the Investment Manager (the &#147;Procedures&#148;), the amount of the commission it has received and that the amount of such compensation is permissible
under the Procedures. This authorization is executed and delivered pursuant to Section&nbsp;11(a) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 and Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">11a2-2(T)</FONT> under that Act. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5.&nbsp;<U>Conduct of the Investment Manager</U>. All actions engaged in by the Investment Manager under this Agreement will at all times
conform to and be in accordance with the requirements imposed by: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) any provisions of applicable law;
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) such policies and procedures as may be adopted from time to time by the Board of Trustees, provided that
the Investment Manager will not be obligated to follow any such policies or procedures that increases its obligations, responsibilities or liabilities until it has received actual notice of the policy or procedure. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">6.&nbsp;<U>Reimbursement of Legal and Other Professional Expenses</U>. The Investment Manager, in its discretion, may rely upon the
advice of legal counsel, independent accountants and other professional advisors to the Fund in connection with the performance of its activities on behalf of the Fund under this Agreement, and the Fund shall bear full responsibility therefor and
the expense of any fees and disbursements arising from the use of such professional advisors. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">7.&nbsp;<U>Fees</U>.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The Fund shall pay the Investment Manager as full compensation for the services performed by the
Investment Manager a fee of 1.00%&nbsp;per year (the &#147;Management Fee&#148;) payable monthly at a rate of 1/12 of 1.00% of the Fund&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">month-end</FONT> net asset value, before giving effect to repurchases,
repurchase fees (if any), and after giving effect to other expenses. The Management Fee shall be appropriately prorated in the event that this Agreement becomes effective as of a date other than the beginning of a month or terminates as of a date
other than the end of a month. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) Payment of the Management Fee shall be made monthly in arrears within 30
days of the calculation of the Fund&#146;s net asset value each month. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-3
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c) Each payment for services to the Investment Manager shall be accompanied
by a report of the Fund, prepared either by the Fund&#146;s administrator or by an established firm of independent public accountants, which shows the amount properly payable to the Investment Manager under this Agreement, and the manner of
computation thereof. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">8.&nbsp;<U>Expenses of the Fund</U>. The Fund will pay or assume all ordinary operating expenses of the
Fund, other than expenses assumed by the Investment Manager. Expenses to be borne by the Fund include, without limitation (i)&nbsp;organizational costs, (ii)&nbsp;SEC fees or other regulatory fees; (iii)&nbsp;industry association fees;
(iv)&nbsp;costs of independent pricing services; (v)&nbsp;all expenses related to its investment program, (vi)&nbsp;all costs and expenses associated with the establishment of Separately Managed Accounts (as defined in the Fund&#146;s Private
Placement Memorandum) (whether or not consummated); (vii)&nbsp;any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-investment</FONT> related interest expense, (viii)&nbsp;outside auditing and legal expenses; (ix)&nbsp;fees paid and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> expenses reimbursed to the Fund&#146;s administrator, custodian, transfer and dividend disbursing agents; (x)&nbsp;escrow and other recordkeeping fees and
expenses; (xi)&nbsp;costs of errors and omissions/directors&#146; and officers&#146; liability insurance and a fidelity bond; (xii)&nbsp;Trustees&#146; fees; (xiii)&nbsp;advisory fees; (xiv)&nbsp;costs of preparing and mailing shareholder reports
and other communications and shareholder meetings; (xv)&nbsp;costs of preparing and printing copies of the Private Placement Memorandum for regulatory purposes and for distribution to existing Shareholders; (xvi)&nbsp;costs and charges for equipment
or services used in communicating information regarding the Fund&#146;s transactions among the Investment Manager and any custodian or other agent engaged by the Fund; (xvii)&nbsp;fees paid and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> expenses reimbursed for fund accounting and investor services; and (xviii)&nbsp;any extraordinary expenses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">9.&nbsp;<U>Expenses of the Investment Manager</U>. The Investment Manager will bear all of its own costs incurred in providing investment advisory services to the Fund, including travel and other expenses
related to the selection and monitoring of Portfolio Managers, as well as its other ordinary operating expenses. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">10.&nbsp;<U>Representations and Warranties</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) The Investment Manager represents and warrants that: (i)&nbsp;it has obtained all applicable licenses, permits, registrations, memberships and approvals that may be required in order to serve in its
designated capacities with respect to this Agreement, and will continue to keep current those licenses, permits, registrations, memberships and approvals for so long as this Agreement is in effect; (ii)&nbsp;it is in material compliance with all
requirements of applicable federal securities and commodities laws, regulations and rules, including the regulations and rules of the SEC, the Commodities Futures Trading Commission and all other laws, rules or regulations applicable to it or its
activities; (iii)&nbsp;it will immediately notify the Fund of the occurrence of any event that would disqualify it from serving in its designated capacities with respect to this Agreement; (iv)&nbsp;it has the capacity and authority to perform its
obligations under this Agreement; (v)&nbsp;this Agreement has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered on behalf of the Investment Manager and is a valid and binding agreement of the Investment Manager enforceable in accordance with
its terms; and (vi)&nbsp;entry into this Agreement will not breach or cause to be breached any undertaking, agreement, contract, statute, rule or regulation to which it is a party or by which it is bound which would materially limit or affect the
performance of its duties under this Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) The Fund represents and warrants that: (i)&nbsp;it is a
statutory trust duly formed and validly existing under the laws of the State of Delaware and has full power and authority to perform its obligations under this Agreement; (ii)&nbsp;it has the capacity and authority to enter into this Agreement;
(iii)&nbsp;this Agreement has been duly and validly authorized, executed and delivered on behalf of the Fund and is a valid and binding agreement of the Fund enforceable in accordance with its terms; and (iv)&nbsp;entry into this Agreement will not
breach or cause to be breached any undertaking, agreement, contract, statute, rule or regulation to which it is a party or by which it is bound that would materially limit or affect the performance of its duties under this Agreement. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">11.&nbsp;<U>Liability of Investment Manager</U>. In the absence of (a)&nbsp;willful misfeasance, bad faith or gross negligence on the
part of the Investment Manager in performance of its obligations and duties under this Agreement, </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-4
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
(b)&nbsp;reckless disregard by the Investment Manager of its obligations and duties under this Agreement, or (c)&nbsp;a loss resulting from a breach of fiduciary duty with respect to the receipt
of compensation for services (in which case any award of damages will be limited to the period and the amount set out in Section&nbsp;36(b)(3) of the 1940 Act), the Investment Manager will not be subject to any liability whatsoever to the Fund, or
to any Shareholder of the Fund for any error of judgment, mistake of law or any other act or omission in the course of, or connected with, rendering services under this Agreement including, without limitation, for any losses that may be sustained in
connection with the purchase, holding, redemption or sale of any security on behalf of the Fund. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">12.&nbsp;<U>Indemnification</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) To the fullest extent permitted by law, the Fund will, subject to Section&nbsp;12(c) of this Agreement, indemnify the Investment Manager (including for this purpose each officer, director, member,
partner, principal, employee or agent of, or any person who controls, is controlled by or is under common control with, the Investment Manager, and their respective executors, heirs, assigns, successors or other legal representatives) (each such
person being referred to as an &#147;indemnitee&#148;) against all losses, claims, damages, liabilities, costs and expenses (&#147;Losses,&#148; and individually, a &#147;Loss&#148;) arising by reason of being or having been Investment Manager to
the Fund, or the past or present performance of services to the Fund in accordance with this Agreement by the indemnitee, except to the extent that the Loss has been determined in a final judicial decision on the merits from which no further right
of appeal may be taken in any action, suit, investigation or other proceeding, whether civil or criminal (&#147;Action&#148;), to have been incurred or suffered by the indemnitee by reason of willful misfeasance, bad faith, gross negligence, or
reckless disregard of the duties involved in the conduct of the indemnitee&#146;s office (&#147;disabling conduct&#148;). Losses include, but are not limited to, amounts paid in satisfaction of judgments, in compromise, or as fines or penalties, and
counsel fees and expenses incurred in connection with the defense or disposition of any Action before any judicial, arbitral, administrative or legislative body, in which the indemnitee may be or may have been involved as a party or otherwise, or
with which the indemnitee may be or may have been threatened, while in office or thereafter. The rights of indemnification provided under this Section&nbsp;12 are not to be construed so as to provide for indemnification of an indemnitee for any
liability (including liability under U.S. federal securities laws that, under certain circumstances, impose liability even on persons that act in good faith) to the extent (but only to the extent) that indemnification of such liability would be in
violation of applicable law, but will be construed so as to effectuate the applicable provisions of this Section&nbsp;12. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) Expenses, including counsel fees and expenses, incurred by any indemnitee (but excluding amounts paid in satisfaction of judgments, in compromise, or as fines or penalties) may be paid from time to
time by the Fund in advance of the final disposition of any Action upon receipt of an undertaking by or on behalf of the indemnitee to repay to the Fund amounts paid if a determination is made that indemnification of the expenses is not authorized
under Section&nbsp;12(a) of this Agreement, so long as (1)&nbsp;the indemnitee provides security for the undertaking, (2)&nbsp;the Fund is insured by or on behalf of the indemnitee against Losses arising by reason of the indemnitee&#146;s failure to
fulfill his, her or its undertaking, or (3)&nbsp;a majority of the trustees (each, a &#147;Trustee,&#148; and collectively, the &#147;Trustees&#148;) of the Fund who are not &#147;interested persons&#148; (as that term is defined in the 1940 Act)
(&#147;Independent Trustees&#148;) (excluding any Trustee who is either seeking advancement of expenses under this Agreement or is or has been a party to any other Action involving claims similar to those involved in the Action giving rise to a
claim for advancement of expenses under this Agreement) or independent legal counsel in a written opinion determines, based on a review of readily available facts (as opposed to a full trial-type inquiry), that reason exists to believe that the
indemnitee ultimately will be entitled to indemnification. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c) With respect to the disposition of any Action
(whether by a compromise payment, pursuant to a consent decree or otherwise) without a final decision on the merits by a court, or by any other body before which the Action has been brought, that an indemnitee was liable to the Fund or its
Shareholders by reason of disabling conduct, indemnification will be provided in accordance with Section&nbsp;12(a) of this Agreement if (1)&nbsp;the indemnification is approved as in the best interests of the Fund by a majority of the Independent
Trustees (excluding any Trustee who is either seeking indemnification under this Agreement or is or has </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-5
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
been a party to any other Action involving claims similar to those involved in the Action giving rise to a claim for indemnification under this Agreement) upon a determination, based upon a
review of readily available facts (as opposed to a full trial-type inquiry), that the indemnitee acted in good faith and in the reasonable belief that the actions were in the best interests of the Fund and that the indemnitee is not liable to the
Fund or its Shareholders by reason of disabling conduct, or (2)&nbsp;the Trustees secure a written opinion of independent legal counsel, based upon a review of readily available facts (as opposed to a full trial-type inquiry), to the effect that
indemnification would not protect the indemnitee against any liability to the Fund or its Shareholders to which the indemnitee would otherwise be subject by reason of disabling conduct. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d) Any indemnification or advancement of expenses made in accordance with this Section&nbsp;12 will not prevent the
recovery from any indemnitee of any amount if the indemnitee subsequently is determined in a final judicial decision on the merits in any Action involving the liability or expense that gave rise to the indemnification or advancement of expenses to
be liable to the Fund or its Shareholders by reason of disabling conduct. In any suit brought by an indemnitee to enforce a right to indemnification under this Section&nbsp;12, it will be a defense that the indemnitee has not met the applicable
standard of conduct described in this Section&nbsp;12. In any suit in the name of the Fund to recover any indemnification or advancement of expenses made in accordance with this Section&nbsp;12 the Fund will be entitled to recover the expenses upon
a final adjudication from which no further right of appeal may be taken. In any suit brought to enforce a right to indemnification or to recover any indemnification or advancement of expenses made in accordance with this Section&nbsp;12, the burden
of proving that the indemnitee is not entitled to be indemnified, or to any indemnification or advancement of expenses, under this Section&nbsp;12 will be on the Fund (or on any Shareholder acting derivatively or otherwise on behalf of the Fund or
its Shareholders). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(e) An indemnitee may not satisfy any right of indemnification or advancement of expenses
granted in this Section&nbsp;12 or to which he, she or it may otherwise be entitled except out of the assets of the Fund, and no Shareholder will be personally liable with respect to any such claim for indemnification or advancement of expenses.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(f) The rights of indemnification provided in this Section&nbsp;12 will not be exclusive of or affect any
other rights to which any person may be entitled by contract or otherwise under law. Nothing contained in this Section&nbsp;12 will affect the power of the Fund to purchase and maintain liability insurance on behalf of the Investment Manager or any
other indemnitee. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">13.&nbsp;<U>Activities of the Investment Manager and Others</U>. The Investment Manager and its affiliates
may engage, simultaneously with their investment management activities on behalf of the Fund, in other businesses and make investments for their own accounts, and may render services similar to those described in this Agreement for other
individuals, companies, trusts or persons, and shall not by reason of such engaging in other businesses, making such investments or rendering of services for others be deemed to be acting in conflict with the interests of the Fund. Notwithstanding
the foregoing, the Investment Manager shall devote sufficient time to the management of the Fund&#146;s assets as is necessary to supervise the investment activities of the Fund. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">14.&nbsp;<U>Permissible Interests</U>. Subject to and in accordance with the Declaration of Trust and the organizational documents of the
Investment Manager (the &#147;Investment Manager Organizational Documents&#148;), (a)&nbsp;Trustees (other than those identified as &#147;disinterested&#148; in the Fund&#146;s Private Placement Memorandum), officers, employees, agents and
Shareholders of the Fund are or may be interested in the Investment Manager (or any successor thereof) as directors, officers, agents, shareholders or otherwise; (b)&nbsp;directors, officers, employees, agents and shareholders of the Investment
Manager are or may be interested in the Fund as Trustees (other than those identified as &#147;disinterested&#148; in the Fund&#146;s Private Placement Memorandum), officers, Shareholders or otherwise; and (c)&nbsp;the Investment Manager (or any
successor) is or may be interested in the Fund as a Shareholder or otherwise. The effect of any such interrelationships will be governed by the Declaration of Trust, the Investment Manager Organizational Documents, the provisions of the 1940 Act and
the provisions of the Investment Advisers Act of 1940. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">D-6

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">15.&nbsp;<U>Term</U>. This Agreement will become effective as of the date first written
above and will continue for an initial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-year</FONT> term, and will continue thereafter so long as the continuance is specifically approved at least annually in conformity with the requirements of the 1940 Act;
<U>provided</U>&nbsp;<U>however</U>, that if the Shareholders of the Fund fail to approve the Agreement as provided in this Section&nbsp;15, the Investment Manager may continue to serve in such capacity in the manner and to the extent permitted by
the 1940 Act and the rules under that Act. This Agreement may be terminated by the Fund at any time, without the payment of any penalty, by vote of a majority of the Board of Trustees or by vote of a majority of the outstanding voting securities of
the Fund on 60 days&#146; written notice to the Investment Manager. This Agreement may be terminated by the Investment Manager at any time, without the payment of any penalty, upon 60 days&#146; written notice to the Fund. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">16. <U>Use of Name</U>. The Fund acknowledges that it adopted its name through the permission of the Investment Manager. The Investment
Manager hereby consents to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exclusive</FONT> use by the Fund of &#147;J.P. Morgan&#148; in its name only so long as the Investment Manager or one of its affiliates serves as the investment manager of the Fund.
The Fund agrees to indemnify and hold harmless the Investment Manager and its affiliates from and against any and all costs, losses, claims, damages or liabilities, joint or several, including, without limitation, attorney&#146;s fees and
disbursements, which may arise out of the Fund&#146;s use or misuse of the name &#147;J.P. Morgan Access Multi-Strategy Fund II&#148; or out of any breach of or failure to comply with this Section&nbsp;16. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">17.&nbsp;<U>Miscellaneous</U>. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT

&#147;assignment,&#148; &#147;interested persons,&#148; and a &#147;vote of a majority of the outstanding voting securities&#148; will have the respective meanings set forth in Section&nbsp;2(a)(4), Section&nbsp;2(a)(19) and Section&nbsp;2(a)(42) of
the 1940 Act, and relevant interpretations of those sections. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b)&nbsp;<U>Notices</U>. Any notice, consent or

of this Agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(j)&nbsp;<U>Fund Obligations</U>. The parties to this Agreement agree that the obligations

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">E-1
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_13"></A>APPENDIX F </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A<SMALL>UDIT</SMALL> <SMALL>AND</SMALL> V<SMALL>ALUATION</SMALL> C<SMALL>OMMITTEE</SMALL> C<SMALL>HARTER</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>JPMORGAN FUNDS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>AUDIT AND VALUATION COMMITTEE CHARTER </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>O<SMALL>RGANIZATION</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">There shall be a committee of the Boards of Trustees</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> (the &#147;Boards&#148;) of the JPMorgan Funds (the &#147;Funds&#148;) known as Audit and Valuation Committee (the
&#147;Committee&#148;). The Committee shall be composed of trustees who: (1)&nbsp;are not &#147;interested persons&#148; of the Funds as defined in Section&nbsp;2(a)(19) of the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended (the &#147;1940 Act&#148;)
(&#147;Independent Trustees&#148;); (2) do not accept, directly or indirectly, any compensation from the Funds or its affiliates, except compensation for services as a member of the Boards or the Boards&#146; committees; and (3)&nbsp;are independent
under applicable requirements of any exchange on which a Fund&#146;s shares are listed. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Each member shall be found by the Independent
Trustees to be free of any relationship that would interfere with their exercise of independent judgment as a Committee member. Each member of the Committee must be &#147;financially literate,&#148; that is, be able to read and understand
fundamental financial statements, including a balance sheet, income statement and cash flow statement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Chairperson of the Boards shall:
(i)&nbsp;determine the number of Committee members, which shall be at least three members; (ii)&nbsp;nominate the members of the Committee; and (iii)&nbsp;appoint the Chairperson of the Committee, subject to the approval of the Boards. The
Chairperson of the Committee shall set the agenda for, and preside at, each meeting of the Committee and shall engage in such other activities on behalf of the Committee as determined from time to time by the Committee or as is consistent with
current practice. The Boards or the Committee may establish subcommittees as the Boards or Committee determines appropriate. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee
shall recommend that the Boards designate one or more Committee members as &#147;Audit Committee Financial Experts&#148; (&#147;ACFE&#148;). Such person(s) shall also be presumed to satisfy any similar listing standards or other regulations
applicable to any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund listed on an exchange. In recommending that a person be designated an ACFE, the Committee shall consider the factors prescribed by Section&nbsp;407 of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act
of 2002 (&#147;Sarbanes-Oxley&#148;), relevant regulations of the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;Commission&#148;) , and such other factors as the Committee deems relevant. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A Committee member designated as ACFE shall not be subject to a different or higher degree of individual responsibility, care or obligation than other members of the Committee. The designation of one or
more Committee members as ACFE shall not alter or decrease the duties and obligations of members of the Committee not so designated. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>M<SMALL>EETINGS</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee
shall meet periodically, but at least quarterly, either on its own or in conjunction with the full Boards, and from time to time as necessary. Meetings of the Committee may be held in person, by video conference or by conference telephone. Where
appropriate, the Committee may take action by unanimous written consent in lieu of a meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>R<SMALL>EPORTING</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee Chairperson shall report to the Boards of Trustees and make recommendations as the Committee deems appropriate. The Committee will keep
minutes of its meetings and will make such minutes available to the </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:8px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:2px;border-bottom:0.5pt solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">1</SUP>&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The term &#147;Board of Trustees&#148; also refers to &#147;Board of Directors&#148; and the term &#147;trustee&#148; also refers to
&#147;director.&#148; </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">F-1
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">
Boards for review. Fund management and members of the Committee who have valuation discussions between Committee meetings shall report on such matters to the full Committee at its next meeting.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>P<SMALL>URPOSES</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The primary purposes of the Committee are to: (1)&nbsp;handle the appointment, retention, compensation, and oversight of the Funds&#146; independent
accountants; (2)&nbsp;oversee the performance of the Funds&#146; audit, accounting and financial reporting policies, practices and internal controls; (3)&nbsp;review and approve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services, as required
by the statutes and regulations administered by the Commission, including the 1940 Act and Sarbanes-Oxley; and (4)&nbsp;oversee compliance with the requirements of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K</FONT> and any listing requirements
or market regulations applicable to any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund listed on an exchange. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>A<SMALL>UDIT</SMALL></U><SMALL></SMALL></B><SMALL></SMALL> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee will oversee the quality and objectivity of the Funds&#146; independent audit and the financial statements of the Funds, act as a liaison between the Boards and the Funds&#146; independent
accountants and periodically report to the Boards. In performing its duties, the Committee shall have unrestricted access to each Fund&#146;s independent accountants and executive and financial management of the Funds, and such other resources as it
may deem appropriate. The independent accountant shall report directly to the Committee. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The existence and activities of the Committee shall
not relieve management of any responsibilities to maintain appropriate systems for accounting, internal control and internal audit, nor the Funds&#146; independent accountants of their responsibilities under applicable professional and legal
standards. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>V<SMALL>ALUATION</SMALL> </U> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall be charged with assisting the Boards in their oversight of the valuation of Funds&#146; securities by the Funds&#146; administrator (the &#147;Administrator&#148;), with assistance
from the Funds&#146; investment adviser (the &#147;Adviser&#148;) and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-Advisers</FONT> (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Sub-Advisers&#148;),</FONT> and such other responsibilities as shall be determined
by the Chairperson of the Boards, subject to the approval of the Boards. The Committee hereby delegates authority to the Chairperson of the Committee or any designated member of the Committee to have discussions with Fund management and respond to
inquiries on valuation matters that occur between meetings of the Committee. The Committee shall consult with and report to the Audit Committee and the Chairperson of the Boards. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Funds have adopted certain valuation procedures and have appointed the Administrator, with assistance from the Adviser and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisers,</FONT> the responsibility for
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> operational aspects of the valuation process. In those instances where the valuation procedures or the law require the action of the Committee or the
Boards, the Chairperson of the Committee or any designated member of the Committee shall act in lieu of the Committee or Boards in those instances where it may be impracticable or impossible to hold meetings of the Committee or the Boards. Any such
interim actions taken by a Committee member with respect to valuation shall be submitted to the Committee or the Boards, as appropriate or required, for ratification at the next scheduled meeting of the Committee or the Boards. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall consult with the independent auditor and/or counsel to the Independent Trustees to stay apprised of regulatory developments affecting
valuation issues. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>R<SMALL>ESPONSIBILITIES</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall have the following responsibilities: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Approve the appointment and compensation of the Funds&#146; independent accountants. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">F-2
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Evaluate the independence of the independent accountants, taking into consideration, among other things, whether the independent accountants provide
any consulting, audit and other services to the manager, the administrator, the distributor, or their affiliates, and receive the independent accountants&#146; specific representations as to their independence. In connection with the evaluation of
their independence, the independent accounting firm shall make a written report to the Committee, in such detail as the Committee may require, regarding all services the firm has provided or proposes to provide to the Funds&#146; Adviser,
administrator, distributor, or their affiliates. It is a responsibility of the Committee to engage actively in a dialogue with the independent accountants with respect to any disclosed relationship or service that may impact the objectivity and
independence of the accountants and to take, or recommend that the full Boards take, appropriate action to oversee independence of auditors. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review the arrangements for and scope of the annual audits of the Funds. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review the Funds&#146; financial statements contained in the annual and other periodic reports to shareholders with Fund management and the independent
accountants and determine whether the independent accountants are satisfied with the disclosure and content of the annual financial statements. In addition, the Committee should obtain representations from Fund management as to its assessment of the
adequacy of accounting policies and procedures. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review the final drafts of the annual financial statements for any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund listed on an exchange,
discuss with management and the independent accountants and decide whether to recommend that the financial statements be included in such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund&#146;s annual report. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Prepare an audit committee report as required by Item 306 of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K</FONT> to be included in the proxy
statements relating to the election of directors with respect to any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund listed on an exchange. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Meet with independent counsel for the Independent Trustees and counsel to the Funds to discuss legal issues that could potentially impact the financial
reporting process. This would include items of industry-wide importance and internal issues such as litigation. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review the form of opinion the independent accountants propose to render to the Boards and shareholders. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Meet periodically with the independent accountants in executive session. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Receive reports regarding the state of financial and audit compliance procedures. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Receive reports of the Adviser regarding the state of the Funds&#146; internal controls and, in the presence of the independent accountants, discuss
these reports with management. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">At least one Committee member shall discuss the status of the annual audit for the Fund with Fund management prior to distribution of the financial
statements to shareholders and shall report to the Committee on such discussions, as necessary. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review and approve recommendations by the Administrator for changes to the Funds&#146; valuation policies for submission to the entire Boards for its
approval, oversee the implementation of the Funds&#146; valuation policies by the Administrator, determine whether to approve the fair value recommendations for specific investments pursuant to the Funds&#146; valuation policies, and review and
approve the Pricing Source Hierarchy for submission to the entire Boards for its approval. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review and act on such other matters as referred to the Committee by the Governance Committee or the Boards. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">F-3
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Periodically, as the Committee deems appropriate, the Committee shall: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consider the effect of any changes in accounting principles or practices proposed by management or the independent accountants.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consider and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approve</FONT> any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services to be provided by the
independent accountants to the Funds or to the Funds&#146; Adviser or &#147;Service Affiliates&#148; (if the service provided by the independent accountant to that Service Affiliate relates directly to the operations and financial reporting of the
Funds) and the fees to be charged for such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services. For purposes of this Audit Committee Charter, Service Affiliates include any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with the
Funds&#146; Adviser that provides ongoing services to the Funds. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review the scope of any internal audits to be performed that impact the operations and financial reporting of the Funds and any related findings of the
internal auditors. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review, as necessary, the impact of any material valuation events on the Funds&#146; financial statements. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Undertake such other investigations and consider such other matters of a financial nature including comments by the Commission or any other regulators
(of the Adviser or the Funds) as the Committee deems appropriate. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Review with the Adviser any comments or criticisms from the Commission or any other regulators related to the financial statements of the Funds as
brought to the attention of the Committee and establish procedures, to the extent necessary, for monitoring the resolution of such issues. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Maintain procedures (a summary of which is attached hereto as Exhibit A) for the confidential, anonymous submission by employees and officers of the
Funds, their affiliates, or any other provider of accounting related services of concerns or complaints regarding any accounting, internal audit controls or audit matter and the retention of records related to the retention and treatment of such
concerns in accordance with the requirements of the Sarbanes Act and to address reports from attorneys or auditors of possible violation of federal or state law or fiduciary duty. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Establish procedures (a copy of which is attached hereto as Exhibit B) for the receipt, retention, and treatment of complaints received by any <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> Fund listed on an exchange, such Fund&#146;s investment adviser, administrator, or any other provider of accounting services related to the Fund, internal accounting controls, or auditing matters.
</FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>R<SMALL>ELIANCE</SMALL> O<SMALL>N</SMALL> S<SMALL>ERVICE</SMALL> P<SMALL>ROVIDERS</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Administrator and Adviser shall inform the Committee of matters requiring Committee oversight as required in this Charter. The Committee may rely on
management and other service providers to supply information reasonably necessary for the Committee to carry out its responsibilities. The Chairperson of the Committee shall be responsible for assuring that each item that is a responsibility of the
Committee shall be placed on the agenda of the Committee for at least one meeting during each year. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>I<SMALL>NDEPENDENT</SMALL>
C<SMALL>OUNSEL</SMALL> <SMALL>OR</SMALL> A<SMALL>DVISERS</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee is authorized to engage independent counsel or other
advisers to assist it in carrying out its responsibilities. The costs of engaging independent counsel or other advisers will be borne by the Funds. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A<SMALL>NNUAL</SMALL> R<SMALL>EVIEW</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee shall review and reassess the
adequacy of this Charter at least once per year. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">F-4
</FONT></P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>A<SMALL>MENDMENTS</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Boards may amend this Charter by a vote, including a vote of a majority of the Independent Trustees. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>L<SMALL>IMITATIONS</SMALL> <SMALL>ON</SMALL> C<SMALL>OMMITTEE</SMALL> R<SMALL>ESPONSIBILITY</SMALL> </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee is not responsible for either the preparation of the financial statements or the auditing of the financial statements. Fund Management has the responsibility for preparing the financial
statements and implementing internal controls, and disclosure controls and procedures, and the independent accountants have the responsibility for auditing the financial statements. The independent accountants also will consider the internal control
over financial reporting for the purpose of determining the nature, timing and extent of their audit procedures; any material weaknesses or significant deficiencies identified during the audit will be communicated to the Committee. The review of the
financial statements by the Committee is not of the same scope or quality as the audit performed by the independent auditors. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The
responsibilities of the Committee do not include reviews of the valuation and calculation of the net asset value of any of the Funds, as this responsibility is central to the oversight role of the Boards as a whole. In addition, subject to the
general oversight responsibility of the Boards, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> responsibility for valuation decisions on behalf of the Funds has been delegated to the Administrator, with
assistance from the Adviser and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisers.</FONT> Accordingly, neither the Committee nor its individual members are in any way responsible for the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> operational aspects of the valuation process. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><A NAME="tx173502_14"></A>APPENDIX G </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>G<SMALL>OVERNANCE</SMALL> C<SMALL>OMMITTEE</SMALL> C<SMALL>HARTER</SMALL> </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>JPMORGAN FUNDS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>GOVERNANCE COMMITTEE CHARTER </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>ORGANIZATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">There shall be a committee of the Boards of Trustees</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1"><SUP
STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex">2</SUP></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"> (the &#147;Boards&#148;) of the JPMorgan Funds (the &#147;Funds&#148;) known as the Governance Committee (the
&#147;Committee&#148;). With respect to any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">closed-end</FONT> fund listed on an exchange, the Committee shall function as the Nominating Committee and Compensation Committee or comparable committee as required by
applicable listing standards. The Committee shall be composed solely of trustees who are not &#147;interested persons&#148; of the Funds as defined as defined in Section&nbsp;2(a)(19) of the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended (the &#147;1940
Act&#148;) (&#147;Independent Trustees&#148;). The Chairperson of the Boards shall serve as Chairperson of the Committee. The Chairperson of the Boards shall also determine the number of Committee members and nominate the members of the Committee,
subject to the approval of the Boards. The Chairperson of the Committee shall set the agenda for, and preside at, each meeting of the Committee and shall engage in such other activities on behalf of the Committee as shall be determined from time to
time by the Committee or as is consistent with current practice. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>MEETINGS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Committee may meet either on its own or in conjunction with meetings of the Boards. Meetings of the Committee may be held in person, by video conference or by conference telephone. Where appropriate,
the Committee may take action by unanimous written consent in lieu of a meeting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>RESPONSIBILITIES </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The duties of the Committee are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">&nbsp;</P>
